The river view room is more expensive than the mountain view room and there is no breakfast, which is not worth it. The view is very good during the day, but you can't see anything at night without turning on the lights by the river. You have to go out to play during the day, so there is no need to spend an extra hundred yuan to stay in the river view room. It's a loss, and the cost performance is very low.
I called to ask for a few more bottles of water and they said they could only send two bottles, which is a bit stingy. I ordered a takeaway and they said they would help to deliver it. It took almost an hour, which is really outrageous. They said they couldn't wait and asked me to go down and get it myself. After all, it's a five-star hotel. This service is very disappointing. . .
When checking out, they said they wanted to delay the check-out and agreed very quickly. This is a good comment.
The room hygiene and other things are OK, the sound insulation is OK, the location is in the center, within two kilometers of the business district and scenic spots, it is very convenient to travel, and there are ground and underground parking lots.
In general, the stay is OK, the service is average, there is no need to stay in the river view room, it's a waste of money.
